NOTICE
NO LEGAL RESPONSIBILITY IS ACCEPTED FOR THE PUBLICATION OF ADVERTISEMENTS REGARDING
CHANGE OF NAME IN THE TAMIL NADU GOVERNMENT GAZETTE. PERSONS NOTIFYING THE CHANGES
WILL REMAIN SOLELY RESPONSIBLE FOR THE LEGAL CONSEQUENCES AND ALSO FOR ANY OTHER
MISREPRESENTATION, ETC.
(By Order)

Director of Stationery and Printing.

PUBLIC NOTICE
IN THE MATTER OF COMPANIES ACT, 1956
IN THE MATTER OF NATURE REMEDIES PRIVATE LIMITED
At an Extraordinary General Meeting of the Company held on 7th November, 2014 at the Registered Office
at 75/47, Fourth Avenue, Ashok Nagar, Chennai-600 083, the following resolution was passed to voluntarily wind up
NATURE REMEDIES PRIVATE LIMITED.
RESOLVED THAT having regard to the declaration of solvency dated 10th October 2014, made by the Board of
Directors of the Company under Section 488 of the Companies Act, 1956, stating that the Company would be able to pay
its debts in full within a period of three years from the date of declaration thereof, the Company, having its Registered Office
at 75/47, Fourth Avenue, Ashok Nagar, Chennai-600 083, be wound up voluntarily, pursuant to Section 484 (1) (b) of the
Companies Act, 1956.
Chennai,
7th November 2014.

R.P. KRISHNAMMACHARI,
Director.
